style="text-indent:-0.9em;margin-left:1.2em;font-weight:normal;">&#8226;&#160;Total</div></th><td>$115 million (<a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_by_GDP_(PPP)" title="List of countries by GDP (PPP)">220th</a>)</td></tr><tr class="mergedbottomrow"><th scope="row"><div style="text-indent:-0.9em;margin-left:1.2em;font-weight:normal;">&#8226;&#160;Per capita</div></th><td>$2,900<sup>a</sup> (<a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_by_GDP_(PPP)_per_capita" title="List of countries by GDP (PPP) per capita">195th</a>)</td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Currency</th><td><a href="/wiki/United_States_dollar" title="United States dollar">United States dollar</a> (<a href="/wiki/ISO_4217" title="ISO 4217">USD</a>)</td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Time zone</th><td><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/Coordinated_Universal_Time" title="Coordinated Universal Time">UTC</a>+12</span> (MHT)</td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Date format</th><td>MM/DD/YYYY</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Left-_and_right-hand_traffic" title="Left- and right-hand traffic">Driving side</a></th><td>right</td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Calling code</th><td><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%2B692" title="+692">+692</a></td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/ISO_3166" title="ISO 3166">ISO 3166 code</a></th><td><a href="/wiki/ISO_3166-2:MH" title="ISO 3166-2:MH">MH</a></td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Country_code_top-level_domain" title="Country code top-level domain">Internet TLD</a></th><td><a href="/wiki/.mh" title=".mh">.mh</a></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><div style="text-align:left;margin-left:auto; margin-right:auto;"><ol style="list-style-type: lower-alpha; margin-left: 1em; font-size:90%;">\n<li value="1">2005 estimate.</li>\n</ol></div></td></tr></tbody></table>\n<p>The <b>Marshall Islands</b>, officially the <b>Republic of the Marshall Islands</b> (<a href="/wiki/Marshallese_language" title="Marshallese language">Marshallese</a>: <i lang="mh">Aolep&#257;n Aor&#333;kin M&#807;aje&#316;</i>),<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6"><a href="#cite_note-6">[note 1]</a></sup> are an <a href="/wiki/Island_country" title="Island country">island country</a> and a <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> <a href="/wiki/Associated_state" title="Associated state">associated state</a> near the <a href="/wiki/Equator" title="Equator">equator</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Pacific_Ocean" title="Pacific Ocean">Pacific Ocean</a>, slightly west of the <a href="/wiki/International_Date_Line" title="International Date Line">International Date Line</a>. Geographically, the country is part of the larger island group of <a href="/wiki/Micronesia" title="Micronesia">Micronesia</a>. The country\'s population of 53,158 people (at the 2011 Census<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-autogenerated1_5-1"><a href="#cite_note-autogenerated1-5">[5]</a></sup>) is spread out over 29 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Coral_atoll" title="Coral atoll">coral atolls</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ciafact_2-1"><a href="#cite_note-ciafact-2">[2]</a></sup> comprising 1,156 individual <a href="/wiki/Island" title="Island">islands</a> and <a href="/wiki/Islet" title="Islet">islets</a>.\n</p><p>The islands share <a href="/wiki/Maritime_boundary" title="Maritime boundary">maritime boundaries</a> with the <a href="/wiki/Federated_States_of_Micronesia" title="Federated States of Micronesia">Federated States of Micronesia</a> to the west, <a href="/wiki/Wake_Island" title="Wake Island">Wake Island</a> to the north,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7"><a href="#cite_note-7">[note 2]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Kiribati" title="Kiribati">Kiribati</a> to the southeast, and <a href="/wiki/Nauru" title="Nauru">Nauru</a> to the south. About 27,797 of the islanders (at the 2011 Census) live on <a href="/wiki/Majuro" title="Majuro">Majuro</a>, which contains the <a href="/wiki/Capital_city" title="Capital city">capital</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ciafact_2-2"><a href="#cite_note-ciafact-2">[2]</a></sup> Data from the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> indicates an estimated population in 2016 of 53,066. In 2016, 73.3% of the population were defined as being "urban". The UN also indicates a population density of 295 per km<sup>2</sup> (765 people per mi<sup>2</sup>) and its projected 2020 population is 53,263.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8"><a href="#cite_note-8">[6]</a></sup>\n</p><p>Micronesian colonists reached the Marshall Islands using canoes circa <a href="/wiki/2nd_millennium_BC" title="2nd millennium BC">2nd millennium BC</a>, with interisland navigation made possible using <a href="/wiki/Marshall_Islands_stick_chart" title="Marshall Islands stick chart">traditional stick charts</a>. They eventually settled here.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bbc.com_9-0"><a href="#cite_note-bbc.com-9">[7]</a></sup> Islands in the archipelago were first explored by <a href="/wiki/Ethnic_groups_in_Europe" title="Ethnic groups in Europe">Europeans</a> in the 1520s, starting with <a href="/wiki/Ferdinand_Magellan" title="Ferdinand Magellan">Ferdinand Magellan</a>, a Portuguese at the service of Spain, <a href="/wiki/Juan_Sebasti%C3%A1n_Elcano" title="Juan Sebasti&#225;n Elcano">Juan Sebasti&#225;n Elcano</a> and Miguel de Saavedra. Spanish explorer <a href="/wiki/Alonso_de_Salazar" title="Alonso de Salazar">Alonso de Salazar</a> reported sighting an atoll in August 1526.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bbc.com_9-1"><a href="#cite_note-bbc.com-9">[7]</a></sup> Other expeditions by Spanish and English ships followed. The islands derive their name from British explorer <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/John_Marshall_(British_captain)" title="John Marshall (British captain)">John Marshall</a>, who visited in 1788. The islands were historically known by the inhabitants as "jolet jen Anij" (Gifts from God).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pacificrisa_10-0"><a href="#cite_note-pacificrisa-10">[8]</a></sup>\n</p><p>Spain claimed the islands in 1592, and the European powers recognized its sovereignty over the islands in 1874. They had been part of the <a href="/wiki/Spanish_East_Indies" title="Spanish East Indies">Spanish East Indies</a> formally since 1528. Later, Spain sold some of the islands to the <a href="/wiki/German_Empire" title="German Empire">German Empire</a> in 1885, and they became part of <a href="/wiki/German_New_Guinea" title="German New Guinea">German New Guinea</a> that year, run by the trading companies doing business in the islands, particularly the Jaluit Company.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bbc.com_9-2"><a href="#cite_note-bbc.com-9">[7]</a></sup> In <a href="/wiki/World_War_I" title="World War I">World War I</a> the <a href="/wiki/Empire_of_Japan" title="Empire of Japan">Empire of Japan</a> occupied the Marshall Islands, which in 1920, the <a href="/wiki/League_of_Nations" title="League of Nations">League of Nations</a> combined with other former German territories to form the <a href="/wiki/South_Pacific_Mandate" title="South Pacific Mandate">South Pacific Mandate</a>. During <a href="/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">World War II</a>, the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> took control of the islands in the <a href="/wiki/Gilbert_and_Marshall_Islands_campaign" title="Gilbert and Marshall Islands campaign">Gilbert and Marshall Islands campaign</a> in 1944. Nuclear testing began in 1946 and concluded in 1958.\n</p><p>The US government formed the Congress of Micronesia in 1965, a plan for increased self-governance of Pacific islands. The <a href="/wiki/Trust_Territory_of_the_Pacific_Islands" title="Trust Territory of the Pacific Islands">Trust Territory of the Pacific Islands</a> in 1979 provided independence to the Marshall Islands, whose constitution and president (Amata Kabua) were formally recognized by the US. Full sovereignty or <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Self-government" title="Self-government">Self-government</a> was achieved in a <a href="/wiki/Compact_of_Free_Association" title="Compact of Free Association">Compact of Free Association</a> with the United States. Marshall Islands has been a <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> member state since 1991.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bbc.com_9-3"><a href="#cite_note-bbc.com-9">[7]</a></sup> Politically, the Marshall Islands is a <a href="/wiki/Presidential_system" title="Presidential system">presidential</a> <a href="/wiki/Republic" title="Republic">republic</a> in <a href="/wiki/Associated_state" title="Associated state">free association</a> with the United States, with the US providing defense, subsidies, and access to U.S.-based agencies such as the <a href="/wiki/Federal_Communications_Commission" title="Federal Communications Commission">Federal Communications Commission</a> and the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Postal_Service" title="United States Postal Service">United States Postal Service</a>. With few natural resources, the islands\' wealth is based on a <a href="/wiki/Service_economy" title="Service economy">service economy</a>, as well as some <a href="/wiki/Fishing" title="Fishing">fishing</a> and <a href="/wiki/Agriculture" title="Agriculture">agriculture</a>; aid from the United States represents a large percentage of the islands\' <a href="/wiki/Gross_domestic_product" title="Gross domestic product">gross domestic product</a>. The country uses the <a href="/wiki/United_States_dollar" title="United States dollar">United States dollar</a> as its currency, though it has also created a <a href="/wiki/Cryptocurrency" title="Cryptocurrency">cryptocurrency</a> which it uses as legal tender.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11"><a href="#cite_note-11">[9]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12"><a href="#cite_note-12">[10]</a></sup>\n</p><p>The majority of the citizens of the Republic of Marshall Islands, formed in 1982, are of Marshallese descent, though there are small numbers of immigrants from the United States, China, <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>, and other Pacific islands. The two <a href="/wiki/Official_language" title="Official language">official languages</a> are <a href="/wiki/Marshallese_language" title="Marshallese language">Marshallese</a>, which is one of the <a href="/wiki/Malayo-Polynesian_languages" title="Malayo-Polynesian languages">Malayo-Polynesian languages</a>, and <a href="/wiki/English_language" title="English language">English</a>. Almost the entire population of the islands practices some religion, with three-quarters of the country either following the <a href="/wiki/United_Church_of_Christ_%E2%80%93_Congregational_in_the_Marshall_Islands" title="United Church of Christ &#8211; Congregational in the Marshall Islands">United Church of Christ &#8211; Congregational in the Marshall Islands</a> (UCCCMI) or the <a href="/wiki/Assemblies_of_God" title="Assemblies of God">Assemblies of God</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13"><a href="#cite_note-13">[11]</a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="toc" id="toc"><input class="toctogglecheckbox" id="toctogglecheckbox" role="button" style="display:none" type="checkbox"/><div class="toctitle" 1944</div></div></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Leaving-bikini.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" <b>needs additional citations for <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">verification</a></b>.<span class="hide-when-compact"> Please help <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit">improve this article</a> by <a href="/wiki/Help:Introduction_to_referencing_with_Wiki_Markup/1" title="Help:Introduction to referencing with Wiki Markup/1">adding citations to reliable sources</a>. Unsourced material may be challenged and removed.<br/><small><span class="plainlinks"><i>Find sources:</i>&#160;<a class="external text" href="//www.google.com/search?as_eq=wikipedia&amp;q=%22Marshall+Islands%22" rel="nofollow">"Marshall Islands"</a>&#160;&#8211;&#160;<a class="external text" href="//www.google.com/search?tbm=nws&amp;q=%22Marshall+Islands%22+-wikipedia" rel="nofollow">news</a>&#160;<b>&#183;</b> <a class="external text" href="//www.google.com/search?&amp;q=%22Marshall+Islands%22+site:news.google.com/newspapers&amp;source=newspapers" rel="nofollow">newspapers</a>&#160;<b>&#183;</b> <a class="external text" href="//www.google.com/search?tbs=bks:1&amp;q=%22Marshall+Islands%22+-wikipedia" rel="nofollow">books</a>&#160;<b>&#183;</b> <a class="external text" href="//scholar.google.com/scholar?q=%22Marshall+Islands%22" rel="nofollow">scholar</a>&#160;<b>&#183;</b> <a class="external text" href="https://www.jstor.org/action/doBasicSearch?Query=%22Marshall+Islands%22&amp;acc=on&amp;wc=on" rel="nofollow">JSTOR</a></span></small></span> <small class="date-container"><i>(<span class="date">January 2009</span>)</i></small><small class="hide-when-compact"><i> (<a href="/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal" title="Help:Maintenance template removal">Learn how and when to remove this template message</a>)</i></small></div></td></tr></tbody></table>\n<p>Evidence suggests that around 3,000 years ago successive waves of human migrants from <a href="/wiki/Southeast_Asia" title="Southeast Asia">Southeast Asia</a> spread across the Western <a href="/wiki/Pacific_Ocean" title="Pacific Ocean">Pacific</a> populating its many small islands. The Marshall Islands were settled by <a href="/wiki/Micronesia" title="Micronesia">Micronesians</a> in the 2nd millennium BC. Little is known of the islands\' early history.  Early settlers traveled between the islands by canoe using traditional <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Stick_chart" title="Stick chart">stick charts</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14"><a href="#cite_note-14">[12]</a></sup>\n</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spanish</a> explorer <a href="/wiki/Alonso_de_Salazar" title="Alonso de Salazar">Alonso de Salazar</a> landed there in 1526, and the archipelago came to be known as "<i>Los Pintados</i>" ("The Painted (Ones)", possibly referring to the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Autochthonous_peoples" title="Autochthonous peoples">autochthonous</a> people first found there), "<i>Las Hermanas</i>" ("The Sisters") and "<i>Los Jardines</i>" ("The Gardens") within the <a href="/wiki/Spanish_Empire" title="Spanish Empire">Spanish Empire</a>, first falling within the jurisdiction of the <a href="/wiki/New_Spain" title="New Spain">Viceroyalty of New Spain</a>, to then be administered directly by Madrid (through the <a href="/wiki/Captaincy_General_of_the_Philippines" title="Captaincy General of the Philippines">Captaincy General of the Philippines</a>) upon the <a href="/wiki/Latin_American_wars_of_independence" title="Latin American wars of independence">independence of Latin America</a> and the dissolution of New Spain starting in 1821.\n</p><p>They were only formally possessed by Spain for much of their colonial history, and were generally considered part of the "<a class="external text" href="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/e/e4/Islas_Marianas_Palaos_y_Carolinas.JPG">Carolines</a>" (present-day Federated State of Micronesia, Palau, and the US Territories of Marianas and Guam, as well as the Marshall Islands themselves), or alternatively the "Nuevas Filipinas" ("New Philippines"). The islands were mostly left to their own affairs except for short-lived religious missions (documented in 1668 and 1731) during the 16th and 17th centuries. They were largely ignored by European powers except for cartographic demarcation treaties between the Iberian Empires (Portugal and Castilian Spain) in 1529, 1750 and 1777. The archipelago corresponding to the present-day country was independently named by <a href="/wiki/Adam_Johann_von_Krusenstern" title="Adam Johann von Krusenstern">Krusenstern</a>, after <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Great_Britain" title="Kingdom of Great Britain">British</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Explorer" title="Explorer">explorer</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/John_Marshall_(British_captain)" title="John Marshall (British captain)">John Marshall</a>, who visited them together with <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Thomas_Gilbert_(captain)" title="Thomas Gilbert (captain)">Thomas Gilbert</a> in 1788, en route from <a href="/wiki/Botany_Bay" title="Botany Bay">Botany Bay</a> to <a href="/wiki/Guangzhou" title="Guangzhou">Canton</a> (two ships of the <a href="/wiki/First_Fleet" title="First Fleet">First Fleet</a>), and started establishing German and British trading posts, not formally contested by Spain.\n</p><p>The Marshall Islands were formally claimed by <a href="/wiki/Spanish_Empire" title="Spanish Empire">Spain</a> in 1874 through its capital in the East Indies, <a href="/wiki/Manila" title="Manila">Manila</a>, marking the start of several strategic moves by the <a href="/wiki/German_Empire" title="German Empire">Second Reich</a> during the 1870s and 80s to annex them (claiming them to be "by chance unoccupied"<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15"><a href="#cite_note-15">[13]</a></sup>). This policy would culminate in a tense naval episode in 1885, which did not degenerate into a conflict due to the poor readiness of Spain\'s naval forces and the unwillingness for open military action from the German side.\n</p><p>Following <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Papal" title="Papal">papal</a> mediation and German compensation of $4.5 million, Spain reached an agreement with <a href="/wiki/German_Empire" title="German Empire">Germany</a> in 1885: the 1885 Hispano-German Protocol of Rome. This accord established a <a href="/wiki/Protectorate" title="Protectorate">protectorate</a> and set up trading stations on the islands of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jaluit" title="Jaluit">Jaluit</a> (Jol&#243;) and <a href="/wiki/Ebon_Atoll" title="Ebon Atoll">Ebon</a> to carry out the flourishing <a href="/wiki/Copra" title="Copra">copra</a> (dried <a href="/wiki/Coconut" title="Coconut">coconut</a> meat) trade. Marshallese <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Iroij" title="Iroij">Iroij</a> (high chiefs) continued to rule under indirect colonial German administration, rendered tacitly effective by the wording in the 1885 Protocol, which demarcated an area subject to Spanish sovereignty (0-11&#186;N, 133-164&#186;E) omitting the Eastern Carolines, that is, the Marshall and Gilbert archipelagos, where most of the German trading posts were located.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16"><a href="#cite_note-16">[14]</a></sup> The disputes were rendered moot after the selling of the whole Caroline archipelago to Germany 13 years later.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17"><a href="#cite_note-17">[15]</a></sup>\n</p><p>At the beginning of <a href="/wiki/World_War_I" title="World War I">World War I</a>, <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a> assumed control of the Marshall Islands. The Japanese headquarters was established at the German center of administration, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jaluit" title="Jaluit">Jaluit</a>. On January 31, 1944 American forces landed on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kwajalein" title="Kwajalein">Kwajalein</a> <a href="/wiki/Atoll" title="Atoll">atoll</a> and U.S. Marines and Army troops later took control of the islands from the Japanese on February 3, following intense fighting on Kwajalein and <a href="/wiki/Enewetak_Atoll" title="Enewetak Atoll">Enewetak</a> atolls. In 1947, the United States, as the occupying power, entered into an agreement with the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UN_Security_Council" title="UN Security Council">UN Security Council</a> to administer much of <a href="/wiki/Micronesia" title="Micronesia">Micronesia</a>, including the Marshall Islands, as the <a href="/wiki/Trust_Territory_of_the_Pacific_Islands" title="Trust Territory of the Pacific Islands">Trust Territory of the Pacific Islands</a>.\n</p><p>From 1946 to 1958, it served as the <a href="/wiki/Pacific_Proving_Grounds" title="Pacific Proving Grounds">Pacific Proving Grounds</a> for the United States and was the site of 67 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nuclear_test" title="Nuclear test">nuclear tests</a> on various atolls.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18"><a href="#cite_note-18">[16]</a></sup> The world\'s first <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hydrogen_bomb" title="Hydrogen bomb">hydrogen bomb</a>, codenamed "<a href="/wiki/Ivy_Mike" title="Ivy Mike">Mike</a>", was tested at the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Enewetak" title="Enewetak">Enewetak</a> atoll in the Marshall Islands on November 1, (local date) in 1952, by the United States.\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Castle_Bravo_Blast.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1200" data-file-width="1600" decoding="async" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5d/Castle_Bravo_Blast.jpg/220px-Castle_Bravo_Blast.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5d/Castle_Bravo_Blast.jpg/330px-Castle_Bravo_Blast.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5d/Castle_Bravo_Blast.jpg/440px-Castle_Bravo_Blast.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Castle_Bravo_Blast.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Mushroom cloud from the largest atmospheric <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nuclear_test" title="Nuclear test">nuclear test</a> the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> ever conducted, <a href="/wiki/Castle_Bravo" title="Castle Bravo">Castle Bravo</a>.</div></div></div>\n<p>Nuclear testing began in 1946 on <a href="/wiki/Bikini_Atoll" title="Bikini Atoll">Bikini Atoll</a> after residents were evacuated. Over the years, 67 weapon tests were conducted, including the 15-megaton Castle Bravo hydrogen bomb test, which produced significant fallout in the region. The testing concluded in 1958. Over the years, just one of over 60 islands was cleaned by the US government, and the inhabitants are still waiting for the 2 billion dollars in compensation assessed by the Nuclear Claims Tribunal. Many of the islanders and their descendants still live in exile, as the islands remain contaminated with high levels of radiation.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-theguardian.com_19-0"><a href="#cite_note-theguardian.com-19">[17]</a></sup>\n</p><p>A significant <a href="/wiki/Radar" title="Radar">radar</a> installation was constructed on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kwajalein" title="Kwajalein">Kwajalein</a> atoll.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20"><a href="#cite_note-20">[18]</a></sup>\n</p><p>On May 1, 1979, in recognition of the evolving political status of the Marshall Islands, the United States recognized the constitution of the Marshall Islands and the establishment of the Government of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Republic_of_the_Marshall_Islands" title="Republic of the Marshall Islands">Republic of the Marshall Islands</a>. The constitution incorporates both American and British constitutional concepts.\n</p><p>There have been a number of local and national elections since the Republic of the Marshall Islands was founded. The United Democratic Party, running on a reform platform, won the 1999 parliamentary election, taking control of the presidency and cabinet.\n</p><p>The islands signed a <a href="/wiki/Compact_of_Free_Association" title="Compact of Free Association">Compact of Free Association</a> with the United States in 1986. Trusteeship was ended under <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council_Resolution_683" title="United Nations Security Council Resolution 683">United Nations Security Council Resolution 683</a> of December 22, 1990. Until 1999 the islanders received <a href="/wiki/United_States_dollar" title="United States dollar">US$</a>180M for continued American use of Kwajalein atoll, US$250M in compensation for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nuclear_test" title="Nuclear test">nuclear testing</a>, and US$600M in other payments under the compact.\n</p><p>Despite the constitution, the government was largely controlled by Iroij. It was not until 1999, following <a href="/wiki/Political_corruption" title="Political corruption">political corruption</a> allegations, that the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Aristocracy_(government)" title="Aristocracy (government)">aristocratic</a> government was overthrown, with <a href="/wiki/Imata_Kabua" title="Imata Kabua">Imata Kabua</a> replaced by the <a href="/wiki/Commoner" title="Commoner">commoner</a> <a href="/wiki/Kessai_Note" title="Kessai Note">Kessai Note</a>.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Geography">Geography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Geography">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main articles: <a href="/wiki/Geography_of_the_Marshall_Islands" title="Geography of the Marshall Islands">Geography of the Marshall Islands</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Administrative_divisions_of_the_Marshall_Islands" title="Administrative divisions of the Marshall Islands">Administrative divisions of the Marshall Islands</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Effects_of_climate_change_on_island_nations" title="Effects of climate change on island nations">Effects of climate change on island nations</a></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:MH_-map_A.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:MH_-map_A.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Map of the Marshall Islands</div></div></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:JJ7V2741_(40325750).jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="470" data-file-width="800" Islands</div></div></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Eneko_Islet_12.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1944" data-file-width="2592" decoding="async" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Eneko_Islet_12.JPG/220px-Eneko_Islet_12.JPG" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Eneko_Islet_12.JPG/440px-Eneko_Islet_12.JPG 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Eneko_Islet_12.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Beach scenery at the islet of Eneko, <a href="/wiki/Majuro" title="Majuro">Majuro</a>.</div></div></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Bikini_Atoll_Nuclear_Test_Site-115017.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1728" data-file-width="2592" decoding="async" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9f/Bikini_Atoll_Nuclear_Test_Site-115017.jpg/220px-Bikini_Atoll_Nuclear_Test_Site-115017.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9f/Bikini_Atoll_Nuclear_Test_Site-115017.jpg/330px-Bikini_Atoll_Nuclear_Test_Site-115017.jpg 1.5x, class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Bikini_Atoll_Nuclear_Test_Site-115017.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>View of the coast of <a href="/wiki/Bikini_Atoll" title="Bikini Atoll">Bikini Atoll</a> from above</div></div></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Marshall_Islands_(10700720174).jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2802" data-file-width="3922" decoding="async" height="157" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/69/Marshall_Islands_%2810700720174%29.jpg/220px-Marshall_Islands_%2810700720174%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/69/Marshall_Islands_%2810700720174%29.jpg/330px-Marshall_Islands_%2810700720174%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/69/Marshall_Islands_%2810700720174%29.jpg/440px-Marshall_Islands_%2810700720174%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Marshall_Islands_(10700720174).jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>View of Marshall Islands</div></div></div>\n<p>The Marshall Islands sit atop ancient submerged volcanoes rising from the ocean floor, about halfway between <a href="/wiki/Hawaii" title="Hawaii">Hawaii</a> and <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pacificrisa_10-1"><a href="#cite_note-pacificrisa-10">[8]</a></sup> north of <a href="/wiki/Nauru" title="Nauru">Nauru</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kiribati" title="Kiribati">Kiribati</a>, east of the <a href="/wiki/Federated_States_of_Micronesia" title="Federated States of Micronesia">Federated States of Micronesia</a>, and south of the disputed U.S. territory of <a href="/wiki/Wake_Island" title="Wake Island">Wake Island</a>, to which it also lays claim.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-rmiembassyus.org_21-0"><a href="#cite_note-rmiembassyus.org-21">[19]</a></sup> The atolls and islands form two groups: the <a href="/wiki/Ratak_Chain" title="Ratak Chain">Ratak (sunrise)</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Ralik_Chain" title="Ralik Chain">Ralik (sunset)</a>. The two island chains lie approximately parallel to one another, running northwest to southeast, comprising about 750,000 square miles (1,900,000&#160;km<sup>2</sup>) of ocean but only about 70 square miles (180&#160;km<sup>2</sup>) of land mass.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pacificrisa_10-2"><a href="#cite_note-pacificrisa-10">[8]</a></sup> Each includes 15 to 18 islands and atolls.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-beardslee_22-0"><a href="#cite_note-beardslee-22">[20]</a></sup> The country consists of a total of 29 <a href="/wiki/Atoll" title="Atoll">atolls</a> and five isolated islands situated in about 180,000 square miles (470,000&#160;km<sup>2</sup>) of the Pacific.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-rmiembassyus.org_21-1"><a href="#cite_note-rmiembassyus.org-21">[19]</a></sup> The largest atoll with a land area of 6 square miles (16&#160;km<sup>2</sup>) is Kwajalein. It surrounds a 655-square-mile (1,700&#160;km<sup>2</sup>) lagoon.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23"><a href="#cite_note-23">[21]</a></sup>\n</p><p>Twenty-four of the atolls and islands are inhabited. Atolls are uninhabited due to poor living conditions, lack of rain, or nuclear contamination. The uninhabited atolls are:\n</p>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Ailinginae_Atoll" title="Ailinginae Atoll">Ailinginae Atoll</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Bikar_Atoll" title="Bikar Atoll">Bikar (Bikaar) Atoll</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Bikini_Atoll" title="Bikini Atoll">Bikini Atoll</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Bokak_Atoll" title="Bokak Atoll">Bokak Atoll</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Erikub_Atoll" title="Erikub Atoll">Erikub Atoll</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Jemo_Island" title="Jemo Island">Jemo Island</a></li>\n<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nadikdik_Atoll" title="Nadikdik Atoll">Nadikdik Atoll</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Rongerik_Atoll" title="Rongerik Atoll">Rongerik Atoll</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Toke_Atoll" title="Toke Atoll">Toke Atoll</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Ujelang_Atoll" title="Ujelang Atoll">Ujelang Atoll</a></li></ul>\n<p>The average altitude above sea level for the entire country is 7 feet (2.1&#160;m).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-rmiembassyus.org_21-2"><a href="#cite_note-rmiembassyus.org-21">[19]</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Shark_sanctuary">Shark sanctuary</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Shark sanctuary">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>In October 2011, the government declared that an area covering nearly 2,000,000 square kilometers (772,000&#160;sq&#160;mi) of ocean shall be reserved as a <a href="/wiki/Shark_sanctuary" title="Shark sanctuary">shark sanctuary</a>. This is the world\'s largest shark sanctuary, extending the worldwide ocean area in which sharks are protected from 2,700,000 to 4,600,000 square kilometers (1,042,000 to 1,776,000&#160;sq&#160;mi). In protected waters, all shark fishing is banned and all <a href="/wiki/Bycatch" title="Bycatch">by-catch</a> must be released. However, some have questioned the ability of the Marshall Islands to enforce this zone.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24"><a href="#cite_note-24">[22]</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Territorial_claim_on_Wake_Island">Territorial claim on Wake Island</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Territorial claim on Wake Island">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The Marshall Islands also lays claim to <a href="/wiki/Wake_Island" title="Wake Island">Wake Island</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-25"><a href="#cite_note-25">[23]</a></sup> While Wake has been administered by the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> since 1899, the Marshallese government refers to it by the name <i>Enen-kio</i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26"><a href="#cite_note-26">[24]</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Climate">Climate</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Climate">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:ClimateMajuroMarshallIslands.PNG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="450" data-file-width="450" decoding="async" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dc/ClimateMajuroMarshallIslands.PNG/150px-ClimateMajuroMarshallIslands.PNG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dc/ClimateMajuroMarshallIslands.PNG/225px-ClimateMajuroMarshallIslands.PNG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dc/ClimateMajuroMarshallIslands.PNG/300px-ClimateMajuroMarshallIslands.PNG 2x" width="150"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:ClimateMajuroMarshallIslands.PNG" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Average monthly temperatures (red) and precipitation (blue) on <a href="/wiki/Majuro" title="Majuro">Majuro</a>.</div></div></div>\n<p>The climate has a <a href="/wiki/Dry_season" title="Dry season">dry season</a> from December to April and a <a href="/wiki/Wet_season" title="Wet season">wet season</a> from May to November. Many Pacific <a href="/wiki/Typhoon" title="Typhoon">typhoons</a> begin as tropical storms in the Marshall Islands region, and grow stronger as they move west toward the <a href="/wiki/Mariana_Islands" title="Mariana Islands">Mariana Islands</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>.\n</p><p>Due to its very low elevation, the Marshall Islands are threatened by the potential effects of <a href="/wiki/Sea_level_rise" title="Sea level rise">sea level rise</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27"><a href="#cite_note-27">[25]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28"><a href="#cite_note-28">[26]</a></sup> According to the president of <a href="/wiki/Nauru" title="Nauru">Nauru</a>, the Marshall Islands are the most endangered nation in the world due to flooding from <a href="/wiki/Climate_change" title="Climate change">climate change</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29"><a href="#cite_note-29">[27]</a></sup>\n</p><p>Population has outstripped the supply of freshwater, usually from rainfall. The northern atolls get 50 inches (1,300&#160;mm) of rainfall annually; the southern atolls about twice that. The threat of drought is commonplace throughout the island chains.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30"><a href="#cite_note-30">[28]</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Fauna">Fauna</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Fauna">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main articles: <a href="/wiki/List_of_mammals_of_the_Marshall_Islands" title="List of mammals of the Marshall Islands">List of mammals of the Marshall Islands</a> and <a href="/wiki/List_of_butterflies_of_the_Marshall_Islands" title="List of butterflies of the Marshall Islands">List of butterflies of the Marshall Islands</a></div>\n<p>Crabs include <a href="/wiki/Hermit_crab" title="Hermit crab">hermit crabs</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Coconut_crab" title="Coconut crab">coconut crabs</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cause_31-0"><a href="#cite_note-cause-31">[29]</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Birds">Birds</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Birds">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/List_of_birds_of_the_Marshall_Islands" title="List of birds of the Marshall Islands">List of birds of the Marshall Islands</a></div>\n<p>Most birds found in the Marshall Islands, with the exception of those few introduced by man, are either sea birds or a migratory species.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32"><a href="#cite_note-32">[30]</a></sup> There are about 70 species of birds, including 31 seabirds. 15 of these species actually nest locally. Sea birds include the <a href="/wiki/Black_noddy" title="Black noddy">black noddy</a> and the <a href="/wiki/White_tern" title="White tern">white tern</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-loc_33-0"><a href="#cite_note-loc-33">[31]</a></sup> The only land bird is the <a href="/wiki/House_sparrow" title="House sparrow">house sparrow</a>, introduced by man.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cause_31-1"><a href="#cite_note-cause-31">[29]</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Marine">Marine</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Marine">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<p>There are about 300 species of fish, 250 of which are <a href="/wiki/Coral_reef_fish" title="Coral reef fish">reef fish</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-loc_33-1"><a href="#cite_note-loc-33">[31]</a></sup>\n</p>\n<ul><li>Turtles: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chelonia_mydas" title="Chelonia mydas">green turtles</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Eretmochelys_imbricata" title="Eretmochelys imbricata">hawksbill</a>, <a href="/wiki/Leatherback_sea_turtle" title="Leatherback sea turtle">Leatherback sea turtles</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Olive_ridley_sea_turtle" title="Olive ridley sea turtle">Olive ridley sea turtles</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-34"><a href="#cite_note-34">[32]</a></sup></li>\n<li>Sharks: There are at least 22 shark species including: <a href="/wiki/Blue_shark" title="Blue shark">Blue shark</a>, <a href="/wiki/Silky_shark" title="Silky shark">Silky shark</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bigeye_thresher" title="Bigeye thresher">Bigeye thresher</a> shark, <a href="/wiki/Pelagic_thresher" title="Pelagic thresher">Pelagic thresher</a> shark, <a href="/wiki/Oceanic_whitetip_shark" title="Oceanic whitetip shark">Oceanic whitetip shark</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Tawny_nurse_shark" title="Tawny nurse shark">Tawny nurse shark</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35"><a href="#cite_note-35">[33]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-dos_reis_36-0"><a href="#cite_note-dos_reis-36">[34]</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Insects">Insects</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Insects">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<ul><li>Scorpions: <a href="/wiki/Liocheles_australasiae" title="Liocheles australasiae">dwarf wood scorpion</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Isometrus_maculatus" title="Isometrus maculatus">Common house scorpion</a>. <a href="/wiki/Pseudoscorpion" title="Pseudoscorpion">Pseudoscorpions</a> are occasionally found.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-mii_37-0"><a href="#cite_note-mii-37">[35]</a></sup></li>\n<li>Spiders: Two: a <a href="/wiki/Scytodes" title="Scytodes">scytodes</a>, Dictis striatipes;<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-mii_37-1"><a href="#cite_note-mii-37">[35]</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Jaluiticola" title="Jaluiticola">Jaluiticola</a> a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Genus_(biology)" title="Genus (biology)">genus</a> of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Salticidae" title="Salticidae">jumping spiders</a> endemic to the Marshall Islands. Its only species is <i>Jaluiticola hesslei</i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NMBE_38-0"><a href="#cite_note-NMBE-38">[36]</a></sup></li>\n<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Amphipod" title="Amphipod">Amphipod</a>: One - <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Talorchestia_spinipalma&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Talorchestia spinipalma (page does not exist)">Talorchestia spinipalma</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-mii_37-2"><a href="#cite_note-mii-37">[35]</a></sup></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Orthoptera" title="Orthoptera">Orthoptera</a>: <a href="/wiki/Blattidae" title="Blattidae">cockroaches</a>, <a href="/wiki/American_cockroach" title="American cockroach">American cockroaches</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Short-horned_grasshopper" title="Short-horned grasshopper">short-horned grasshopper</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Gryllidae" title="Gryllidae">crickets</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-mii_37-3"><a href="#cite_note-mii-37">[35]</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Demographics">Demographics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Demographics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Demographics_of_the_Marshall_Islands" title="Demographics of the Marshall Islands">Demographics of the Marshall Islands</a></div>\n<p>Historical population figures are unknown. In 1862, the population was estimated at about 10,000.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-beardslee_22-1"><a href="#cite_note-beardslee-22">[20]</a></sup> In 1960, the entire population was about 15,000. In the 2011 <a href="/wiki/Census" title="Census">Census</a>, the number of island residents was 53,158. Over two-thirds of the population live in the capital, <a href="/wiki/Majuro" title="Majuro">Majuro</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ebeye" title="Ebeye">Ebeye</a>, the secondary urban center, located in <a href="/wiki/Kwajalein_Atoll" title="Kwajalein Atoll">Kwajalein Atoll</a>. This excludes many who have relocated elsewhere, primarily to the United States. The <a href="/wiki/Compact_of_Free_Association" title="Compact of Free Association">Compact of Free Association</a> allows them to freely relocate to the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> and obtain work there.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-gwynne_39-0"><a href="#cite_note-gwynne-39">[37]</a></sup> A large concentration of about 4,300 Marshall Islanders have relocated to <a href="/wiki/Springdale,_Arkansas" title="Springdale, Arkansas">Springdale, Arkansas</a>, the largest population concentration of natives outside their island home.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-40"><a href="#cite_note-40">[38]</a></sup>\n</p><p>Most of the residents are Marshallese, who are of <a href="/wiki/Micronesia" title="Micronesia">Micronesian</a> origin and migrated from <a href="/wiki/Asia" title="Asia">Asia</a> several thousand years ago. A minority of Marshallese have some recent Asian ancestry, mainly <a href="/wiki/Japanese_settlement_in_the_Marshall_Islands" title="Japanese settlement in the Marshall Islands">Japanese</a>. About one-half of the nation\'s population lives on <a href="/wiki/Majuro" title="Majuro">Majuro</a>, the capital, and Ebeye, a densely populated island.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-41"><a href="#cite_note-41">[39]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42"><a href="#cite_note-42">[40]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-43"><a href="#cite_note-43">[41]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Vine2011_44-0"><a href="#cite_note-Vine2011-44">[42]</a></sup> The outer islands are sparsely populated due to lack of employment opportunities and economic development. Life on the outer atolls is generally traditional.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-45"><a href="#cite_note-45">[43]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-46"><a href="#cite_note-46">[44]</a></sup>\n</p><p>The official languages of the Marshall Islands are <a href="/wiki/English_language" title="English language">English</a> and <a href="/wiki/Marshallese_language" title="Marshallese language">Marshallese</a>. Both languages are widely spoken.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-47"><a href="#cite_note-47">[45]</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Religion">Religion</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Religion">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Religion_in_the_Marshall_Islands" title="Religion in the Marshall Islands">Religion in the Marshall Islands</a></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Marshall_Islands_PICT0669_(4776527881).jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1920" data-file-width="2560" decoding="async" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Marshall_Islands_PICT0669_%284776527881%29.jpg/220px-Marshall_Islands_PICT0669_%284776527881%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Marshall_Islands_PICT0669_%284776527881%29.jpg/330px-Marshall_Islands_PICT0669_%284776527881%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Marshall_Islands_PICT0669_%284776527881%29.jpg/440px-Marshall_Islands_PICT0669_%284776527881%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Marshall_Islands_PICT0669_(4776527881).jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Christians in the Marshall Islands</div></div></div>\n<p>Major religious groups in the Republic of the Marshall Islands include the <a href="/wiki/United_Church_of_Christ_%E2%80%93_Congregational_in_the_Marshall_Islands" title="United Church of Christ &#8211; Congregational in the Marshall Islands">United Church of Christ &#8211; Congregational in the Marshall Islands</a>, with 51.5% of the population; the <a href="/wiki/Assemblies_of_God" title="Assemblies of God">Assemblies of God</a>, 24.2%; the <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_(term)" title="Roman Catholic (term)">Roman</a> <a href="/wiki/Catholic_Church" title="Catholic Church">Catholic Church</a>, 8.4%;<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-report_48-0"><a href="#cite_note-report-48">[46]</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/The_Church_of_Jesus_Christ_of_Latter-day_Saints_in_the_Marshall_Islands" title="The Church of Jesus Christ of Latter-day Saints in the Marshall Islands">The Church of Jesus Christ of Latter-day Saints</a> (Mormons), 8.3%.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-report_48-1"><a href="#cite_note-report-48">[46]</a></sup>  Also represented are Bukot Nan Jesus (also known as Assembly of God Part Two), 2.2%; <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Baptist" title="Baptist">Baptist</a>, 1.0%; <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Seventh-day_Adventists" title="Seventh-day Adventists">Seventh-day Adventists</a>, 0.9%; <a href="/wiki/Full_Gospel" title="Full Gospel">Full Gospel</a>, 0.7%; and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Baha%27i_Faith" title="Baha\'i Faith">Baha\'i Faith</a>, 0.6%.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-report_48-2"><a href="#cite_note-report-48">[46]</a></sup> Persons <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nonreligious" title="Nonreligious">without any religious affiliation</a> account for a very small percentage of the population.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-report_48-3"><a href="#cite_note-report-48">[46]</a></sup> There is also a small community of <a href="/wiki/Ahmadiyya" title="Ahmadiyya">Ahmadiyya</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Muslim" title="Muslim">Muslims</a> based in Majuro, with the first mosque opening in the capital in September 2012.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-49"><a href="#cite_note-49">[47]</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Health">Health</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Health">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>See <a href="/wiki/Health_in_the_Marshall_Islands" title="Health in the Marshall Islands">Health in the Marshall Islands</a>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Government">Government</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Government">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Politics_of_the_Marshall_Islands" title="Politics of the Marshall Islands">Politics of the Marshall Islands</a></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Republic_of_the_Marshall_Islands_Capitol_Building.gif"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="116" data-file-width="410" decoding="async" height="62" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0d/Republic_of_the_Marshall_Islands_Capitol_Building.gif/220px-Republic_of_the_Marshall_Islands_Capitol_Building.gif" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0d/Republic_of_the_Marshall_Islands_Capitol_Building.gif/330px-Republic_of_the_Marshall_Islands_Capitol_Building.gif 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/0/0d/Republic_of_the_Marshall_Islands_Capitol_Building.gif 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Republic_of_the_Marshall_Islands_Capitol_Building.gif" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The Marshall Islands Capitol</div></div></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hilda_Heine.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1367" data-file-width="2048" decoding="async" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/Hilda_Heine.jpg/220px-Hilda_Heine.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/Hilda_Heine.jpg/330px-Hilda_Heine.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/Hilda_Heine.jpg/440px-Hilda_Heine.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hilda_Heine.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Hilda_Heine" title="Hilda Heine">H.E. Hilda C. Heine</a>, first woman and current president of the Marshall Islands, walking through the Memorial Amphitheater at <a href="/wiki/Arlington_National_Cemetery" title="Arlington National Cemetery">Arlington National Cemetery</a> Sept. 12, 2017.</div></div></div>\n<p>The government of the Marshall Islands operates under a mixed parliamentary-presidential system as set forth in its Constitution.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-50"><a href="#cite_note-50">[48]</a></sup> Elections are held every four years in <a href="/wiki/Universal_suffrage" title="Universal suffrage">universal suffrage</a> (for all citizens above 18), with each of the twenty-four constituencies (see below) electing one or more representatives (senators) to the lower house of RMI\'s unicameral legislature, the <b><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nitijela" title="Nitijela">Nitijela</a></b>. (<a href="/wiki/Majuro" title="Majuro">Majuro</a>, the capital atoll, elects five senators.) The President, who is head of state as well as head of government, is elected by the 33 senators of the Nitijela. Four of the five Marshallese presidents who have been elected since the Constitution was adopted in 1979 have been traditional <a href="/wiki/Paramount_chief" title="Paramount chief">paramount chiefs</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-mv_51-0"><a href="#cite_note-mv-51">[49]</a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:10.30_%E7%B8%BD%E7%B5%B1%E6%8A%B5%E9%81%94%E9%A6%AC%E7%B4%B9%E7%88%BE%E7%BE%A4%E5%B3%B6%E5%85%B1%E5%92%8C%E5%9C%8B%EF%BC%8C%E7%94%B1%E6%B5%B7%E5%A6%AE%EF%BC%88Hilda_C._Heine%EF%BC%89%E7%B8%BD%E7%B5%B1%E9%99%AA%E5%90%8C%E6%B2%BF%E7%B4%85%E5%9C%B0%E6%AF%AF%E5%89%8D%E9%80%B2%EF%BC%8C%E6%8E%A5%E5%8F%97%E5%85%A9%E5%81%B4%E9%A6%AC%E5%9C%8B%E5%9C%8B%E5%AE%B6%E8%AD%A6%E5%AF%9F%E5%84%80%E9%9A%8A%E8%87%B4%E6%95%AC_(37980845986).jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1365" data-file-width="2048" decoding="async" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ae/10.30_%E7%B8%BD%E7%B5%B1%E6%8A%B5%E9%81%94%E9%A6%AC%E7%B4%B9%E7%88%BE%E7%BE%A4%E5%B3%B6%E5%85%B1%E5%92%8C%E5%9C%8B%EF%BC%8C%E7%94%B1%E6%B5%B7%E5%A6%AE%EF%BC%88Hilda_C._Heine%EF%BC%89%E7%B8%BD%E7%B5%B1%E9%99%AA%E5%90%8C%E6%B2%BF%E7%B4%85%E5%9C%B0%E6%AF%AF%E5%89%8D%E9%80%B2%EF%BC%8C%E6%8E%A5%E5%8F%97%E5%85%A9%E5%81%B4%E9%A6%AC%E5%9C%8B%E5%9C%8B%E5%AE%B6%E8%AD%A6%E5%AF%9F%E5%84%80%E9%9A%8A%E8%87%B4%E6%95%AC_%2837980845986%29.jpg/220px-thumbnail.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ae/10.30_%E7%B8%BD%E7%B5%B1%E6%8A%B5%E9%81%94%E9%A6%AC%E7%B4%B9%E7%88%BE%E7%BE%A4%E5%B3%B6%E5%85%B1%E5%92%8C%E5%9C%8B%EF%BC%8C%E7%94%B1%E6%B5%B7%E5%A6%AE%EF%BC%88Hilda_C._Heine%EF%BC%89%E7%B8%BD%E7%B5%B1%E9%99%AA%E5%90%8C%E6%B2%BF%E7%B4%85%E5%9C%B0%E6%AF%AF%E5%89%8D%E9%80%B2%EF%BC%8C%E6%8E%A5%E5%8F%97%E5%85%A9%E5%81%B4%E9%A6%AC%E5%9C%8B%E5%9C%8B%E5%AE%B6%E8%AD%A6%E5%AF%9F%E5%84%80%E9%9A%8A%E8%87%B4%E6%95%AC_%2837980845986%29.jpg/330px-thumbnail.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ae/10.30_%E7%B8%BD%E7%B5%B1%E6%8A%B5%E9%81%94%E9%A6%AC%E7%B4%B9%E7%88%BE%E7%BE%A4%E5%B3%B6%E5%85%B1%E5%92%8C%E5%9C%8B%EF%BC%8C%E7%94%B1%E6%B5%B7%E5%A6%AE%EF%BC%88Hilda_C._Heine%EF%BC%89%E7%B8%BD%E7%B5%B1%E9%99%AA%E5%90%8C%E6%B2%BF%E7%B4%85%E5%9C%B0%E6%AF%AF%E5%89%8D%E9%80%B2%EF%BC%8C%E6%8E%A5%E5%8F%97%E5%85%A9%E5%81%B4%E9%A6%AC%E5%9C%8B%E5%9C%8B%E5%AE%B6%E8%AD%A6%E5%AF%9F%E5%84%80%E9%9A%8A%E8%87%B4%E6%95%AC_%2837980845986%29.jpg/440px-thumbnail.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:10.30_%E7%B8%BD%E7%B5%B1%E6%8A%B5%E9%81%94%E9%A6%AC%E7%B4%B9%E7%88%BE%E7%BE%A4%E5%B3%B6%E5%85%B1%E5%92%8C%E5%9C%8B%EF%BC%8C%E7%94%B1%E6%B5%B7%E5%A6%AE%EF%BC%88Hilda_C._Heine%EF%BC%89%E7%B8%BD%E7%B5%B1%E9%99%AA%E5%90%8C%E6%B2%BF%E7%B4%85%E5%9C%B0%E6%AF%AF%E5%89%8D%E9%80%B2%EF%BC%8C%E6%8E%A5%E5%8F%97%E5%85%A9%E5%81%B4%E9%A6%AC%E5%9C%8B%E5%9C%8B%E5%AE%B6%E8%AD%A6%E5%AF%9F%E5%84%80%E9%9A%8A%E8%87%B4%E6%95%AC_(37980845986).jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>President Hilda Heine with <a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Taiwan</a> President <a href="/wiki/Tsai_Ing-wen" title="Tsai Ing-wen">Tsai Ing-wen</a> in October 2017</div></div></div>\n<p>In January 2016, senator Hilda Heine was elected by Parliament as the first female president of the Marshall Islands; previous president <a href="/wiki/Casten_Nemra" title="Casten Nemra">Casten Nemra</a> lost office after serving two weeks in a vote of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/No_confidence" title="No confidence">no confidence</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bbc.com_9-4"><a href="#cite_note-bbc.com-9">[7]</a></sup>\n</p><p>Legislative power lies with the Nitijela. The upper house of Parliament, called the <b>Council of Iroij</b>, is an advisory body comprising twelve tribal chiefs. The executive branch consists of the President and the Presidential Cabinet, which consists of ten ministers appointed by the President with the approval of the Nitijela. The twenty-four electoral districts into which the country is divided correspond to the inhabited islands and <a href="/wiki/Atoll" title="Atoll">atolls</a>. There are currently four political parties in the Marshall Islands: <a href="/wiki/Aelon%CC%84_Kein_Ad" title="Aelon&#772; Kein Ad">Aelon&#772; Kein Ad</a> (AKA), <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=United_People%27s_Party_(Marshall_Islands)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="United People\'s Party (Marshall Islands) (page does not exist)">United People\'s Party</a> (UPP), <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Kien_Eo_Am&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Kien Eo Am (page does not exist)">Kien Eo Am</a> (KEA) and <a href="/wiki/United_Democratic_Party_(Marshall_Islands)" title="United Democratic Party (Marshall Islands)">United Democratic Party</a> (UDP). Rule is shared by the AKA and the UDP. The following senators are in the legislative body:\n</p>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Ailinglaplap_Atoll" title="Ailinglaplap Atoll">Ailinglaplap Atoll</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/Christopher_Loeak" title="Christopher Loeak">Christopher Loeak</a> (AKA), Alfred Alfred, Jr. (IND)</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Ailuk_Atoll" title="Ailuk Atoll">Ailuk Atoll</a> &#8211; Maynard Alfred (UDP)</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Arno_Atoll" title="Arno Atoll">Arno Atoll</a> &#8211; Mike Halferty (KEA), Jejwadrik H.
