David Kabua (AKA)</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Wotje_Atoll" title="Wotje Atoll">Wotje Atoll</a> &#8211; Litokwa Tomeing (UPP)</li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Foreign_affairs_and_defense">Foreign affairs and defense</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Foreign affairs and defense">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Marshall_Islands_Police_patrol_vessel_Lomor_and_USCGC_Oliver_Berry_-_180703-G-CA140-115.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="918" data-file-width="1378" decoding="async" height="200" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/65/Marshall_Islands_Police_patrol_vessel_Lomor_and_USCGC_Oliver_Berry_-_180703-G-CA140-115.jpg/300px-Marshall_Islands_Police_patrol_vessel_Lomor_and_USCGC_Oliver_Berry_-_180703-G-CA140-115.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/65/Marshall_Islands_Police_patrol_vessel_Lomor_and_USCGC_Oliver_Berry_-_180703-G-CA140-115.jpg/450px-Marshall_Islands_Police_patrol_vessel_Lomor_and_USCGC_Oliver_Berry_-_180703-G-CA140-115.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/65/Marshall_Islands_Police_patrol_vessel_Lomor_and_USCGC_Oliver_Berry_-_180703-G-CA140-115.jpg/600px-Marshall_Islands_Police_patrol_vessel_Lomor_and_USCGC_Oliver_Berry_-_180703-G-CA140-115.jpg 2x" width="300"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Marshall_Islands_Police_patrol_vessel_Lomor_and_USCGC_Oliver_Berry_-_180703-G-CA140-115.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/USCGC_Oliver_F._Berry_(WPC_1124)" title="USCGC Oliver F. Berry (WPC 1124)">USCGC <i>Oliver Berry</i></a> and the <a href="/wiki/RMIS_Lomor_(03)" title="RMIS Lomor (03)">RMIS <i>Lomor</i></a> on a joint patrol.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Dvids2018-08-01_52-0"><a href="#cite_note-Dvids2018-08-01-52">[50]</a></sup></div></div></div>\n<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Further information: <a href="/wiki/Foreign_relations_of_the_Marshall_Islands" title="Foreign relations of the Marshall Islands">Foreign relations of the Marshall Islands</a> and <a href="/wiki/Compact_of_Free_Association" title="Compact of Free Association">Compact of Free Association</a></div>\n<p>The Compact of Free Association with the United States gives the U.S. sole responsibility for international defense of the Marshall Islands. It gives islanders the right to emigrate to the United States and to work there.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-53"><a href="#cite_note-53">[51]</a></sup>\n</p><p>The Marshall Islands was admitted to the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> based on the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council" title="United Nations Security Council">Security Council</a>\'s recommendation on August 9, 1991, in <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council_Resolution_704" title="United Nations Security Council Resolution 704">Resolution 704</a> and the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_General_Assembly" title="United Nations General Assembly">General Assembly</a>\'s approval on September 17, 1991, in Resolution 46/3.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-54"><a href="#cite_note-54">[52]</a></sup> In international politics within the United Nations, the Marshall Islands has often voted consistently with the United States with respect to General Assembly resolutions.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-55"><a href="#cite_note-55">[53]</a></sup>\n</p><p>On April 28, 2015, the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Iranian_navy" title="Iranian navy">Iranian navy</a> seized the Marshall Island-flagged <a href="/wiki/MV_Maersk_Tigris" title="MV Maersk Tigris">MV <i>Maersk Tigris</i></a> near the <a href="/wiki/Strait_of_Hormuz" title="Strait of Hormuz">Strait of Hormuz</a>. The ship had been chartered by Germany\'s Rickmers Ship Management, which stated that the ship contained no special cargo and no military weapons. The ship was reported to be under the control of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Iranian_Revolutionary_Guard" title="Iranian Revolutionary Guard">Iranian Revolutionary Guard</a> according to <a href="/wiki/The_Pentagon" title="The Pentagon">the Pentagon</a>. Tensions escallated in the region due to the intensifying of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saudi%E2%80%93Yemeni_War" title="Saudi&#8211;Yemeni War">Saudi-led coalition attacks in Yemen</a>. The Pentagon reported that the destroyer <a href="/wiki/USS_Farragut_(DDG-99)" title="USS Farragut (DDG-99)">USS <i>Farragut</i></a> and a maritime reconnaissance aircraft were dispatched upon receiving a distress call from the ship <i>Tigris</i> and it was also reported that all 34 crew members were detained. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/US_Defense_Department" title="US Defense Department">US defense</a> officials have said that they would review U.S. defense obligations to the Government of the Marshall Islands in the wake of recent events and also condemned the shots fired at the bridge as "inappropriate". It was reported in May 2015 that <a href="/wiki/Tehran" title="Tehran">Tehran</a> would release the ship after it paid a penalty.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-56"><a href="#cite_note-56">[54]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-57"><a href="#cite_note-57">[55]</a></sup>\n</p><p>Since 1991 the <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Republic_of_Marshall_Islands_Sea_Patrol&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Republic of Marshall Islands Sea Patrol (page does not exist)">Republic of Marshall Islands Sea Patrol</a>, a division of <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands_Police&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Marshall Islands Police (page does not exist)">Marshall Islands Police</a>, has operated the 160 ton patrol vessel <a href="/wiki/RMIS_Lomor_(03)" title="RMIS Lomor (03)">RMIS <i>Lomor</i></a>. <i>Lomor</i> is one of 22 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pacific_Forum_patrol_vessel" title="Pacific Forum patrol vessel">Pacific Forum patrol vessels</a> <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a> provided to smaller nations in the <a href="/wiki/Pacific_Islands_Forum" title="Pacific Islands Forum">Pacific Forum</a>.  While some other nations\' missions for their vessels include sovereignty, protection, the terms of the Compact of Free Association restrict <i>Lomor</i> to civilian missions, like fishery protection and <a href="/wiki/Search_and_rescue" title="Search and rescue">search and rescue</a>.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Culture">Culture</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Culture">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Culture_of_the_Marshall_Islands" title="Culture of the Marshall Islands">Culture of the Marshall Islands</a></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Marshallese_Rito_Fans.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="335" data-file-width="500" decoding="async" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Marshallese_Rito_Fans.jpg/220px-Marshallese_Rito_Fans.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Marshallese_Rito_Fans.jpg/330px-Marshallese_Rito_Fans.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Marshallese_Rito_Fans.jpg/440px-Marshallese_Rito_Fans.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Marshallese_Rito_Fans.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Marshallese <a href="/wiki/Hand_fan" title="Hand fan">fans</a></div></div></div>\n<p>Although the ancient skills are now in decline, the Marshallese were once able <a href="/wiki/Navigation" title="Navigation">navigators</a>, using the <a href="/wiki/Celestial_navigation" title="Celestial navigation">stars</a> and <a href="/wiki/Marshall_Islands_stick_chart" title="Marshall Islands stick chart">stick-and-shell charts</a>.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Sport">Sport</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Sport">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main articles: <a href="/wiki/Marshall_Islands_Athletics" title="Marshall Islands Athletics">Marshall Islands Athletics</a>, <a href="/wiki/Marshall_Islands_at_the_Olympics" title="Marshall Islands at the Olympics">Marshall Islands at the Olympics</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Category:Sports_in_the_Marshall_Islands" title="Category:Sports in the Marshall Islands">Category: Sports in the Marshall Islands</a></div><p><i>Other sports -</i>\n</p><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Soccer">Soccer</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Soccer">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_football_clubs_in_the_Marshall_Islands" title="List of football clubs in the Marshall Islands">List of football clubs in the Marshall Islands</a></div>\n<p>The Marshall Islands have a small club league, including <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Koober&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Koober (page does not exist)">Koober</a> as the most successful club. I tournament was held by <i>Play Soccer Make Peace</i>. There is a small <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Football_Association" title="Football Association">Football Association</a> on the island of <a href="/wiki/Majuro" title="Majuro">Majuro</a>. The sport of <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">football</a> in its growth is new to the Marshall Islands. The Marshall Islands does not have a <a href="/wiki/Football_team" title="Football team">national football team</a> presently. The Marshall Islands is the only sovereign country in the world that does not have a record of a national football match.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-58"><a href="#cite_note-58">[56]</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span id="Marshall_Islands_Baseball_.2F_Softball_Federation"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Marshall_Islands_Baseball_/_Softball_Federation">Marshall Islands Baseball / Softball Federation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Marshall Islands Baseball / Softball Federation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Softball" title="Softball">Softball</a> and <a href="/wiki/Baseball" title="Baseball">Baseball</a> is held under one sports federation in the Marshall Islands. The President is Jeimata Nokko Kabua. Both sports are growing at a fast pace with hundreds of Marshallese people behind the Marshall Islands Baseball / Softball Federation. The Marshall Islands achieved a <a href="/wiki/Silver_medal" title="Silver medal">silver medal</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Micronesian_Games" title="Micronesian Games">Micronesian Games</a> in 2012, as well as medals in the SPG Games.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-59"><a href="#cite_note-59">[57]</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Economy">Economy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Economy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Economy_of_the_Marshall_Islands" title="Economy of the Marshall Islands">Economy of the Marshall Islands</a></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Marshall_Islands_treemap.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="863" data-file-width="1104" decoding="async" height="172" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/Marshall_Islands_treemap.png/220px-Marshall_Islands_treemap.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/Marshall_Islands_treemap.png/330px-Marshall_Islands_treemap.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/Marshall_Islands_treemap.png/440px-Marshall_Islands_treemap.png 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Marshall_Islands_treemap.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Graphical depiction of Marshall Islands\'s product exports in 28 colour-coded categories.</div></div></div>\n<p>The islands have few natural resources, and their imports far exceed exports. According to the CIA, the value of exports in 2013 was approximately $53.7 million while estimated imports were $133.7 million. Agricultural products include coconuts, tomatoes, melons, taro, breadfruit, fruits, pigs and chickens. Industry is made of the production of copra and craft items, tuna processing and tourism. The GDP in 2016 was an estimated $180 million, with a real growth rate of 1.7%. The GDP per capita was $3,300.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-60"><a href="#cite_note-60">[58]</a></sup>\n</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/International_Monetary_Fund" title="International Monetary Fund">International Monetary Fund</a> reported in mid-2016 that the economy of the Republic had expanded by about 0.5 percent in the Fiscal Year 2015 thanks to an improved fisheries sector. A surplus of 3% of GDP was recorded "owing to record-high fishing license fees. Growth is expected to rise to about 1.5 percent and inflation to about 0.5 percent in FY2016, as the effects of the drought in earlier 2016 are offset by the resumption of infrastructure projects."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imf.org_61-0"><a href="#cite_note-imf.org-61">[59]</a></sup>\n</p><p>In 2018, the Republic of Marshall Islands passed the <a href="/wiki/Sovereign_Currency_Act_of_2018" title="Sovereign Currency Act of 2018">Sovereign Currency Act</a>, which made it the first country to issue their own <a href="/wiki/Cryptocurrency" title="Cryptocurrency">cryptocurrency</a> and certify it as legal tender; the currency is called the "sovereign".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-62"><a href="#cite_note-62">[60]</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Shipping">Shipping</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Shipping">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The Marshall Islands plays a vital role in the international shipping industry as a <a href="/wiki/Flag_of_convenience" title="Flag of convenience">flag of convenience</a> for commercial vessels.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-63"><a href="#cite_note-63">[61]</a></sup> The Marshallese registry began operations in 1990, and is managed through a joint venture with International Registries, Inc., a US-based corporation that has offices in major shipping centers worldwide.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-64"><a href="#cite_note-64">[62]</a></sup> As of 2017, the Marshallese ship registry was the second largest in the world, after that of <a href="/wiki/Panama" title="Panama">Panama</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-65"><a href="#cite_note-65">[63]</a></sup>\n</p><p>Unlike some flag countries, there is no requirement that a Marshallese flag vessel be owned by a Marshallese individual or corporation. Following the 2015 seizure of the <i><a href="/wiki/MV_Maersk_Tigris" title="MV Maersk Tigris">MV Maersk Tigris</a></i>, the United States announced that its treaty obligation to defend the Marshall Islands did not extend to foreign-owned Marshallese flag vessels at sea.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-66"><a href="#cite_note-66">[64]</a></sup>\n</p><p>As a result of ship-to-ship transfers by Marshallese flag tanker vessels, the Marshall Islands have statistically been one of the largest importers of crude oil from the United States, despite the fact that the islands have no oil refining capacity.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-67"><a href="#cite_note-67">[65]</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Labour">Labour</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Labour">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>In 2007, the Marshall Islands joined the <a href="/wiki/International_Labour_Organization" title="International Labour Organization">International Labour Organization</a>, which means its labour laws will comply with international benchmarks. This may impact business conditions in the islands.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-68"><a href="#cite_note-68">[66]</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Taxation">Taxation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Taxation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The <a href="/wiki/Income_tax" title="Income tax">income tax</a> has two brackets, with rates of 8% and 12%.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-rmiparliament.org_69-0"><a href="#cite_note-rmiparliament.org-69">[67]</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Corporate_tax" title="Corporate tax">corporate tax</a> is 3% of revenue.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-rmiparliament.org_69-1"><a href="#cite_note-rmiparliament.org-69">[67]</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Foreign_assistance">Foreign assistance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Foreign assistance">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_government" title="United States government">United States government</a> assistance is the mainstay of the economy. Under terms of the Amended <a href="/wiki/Compact_of_Free_Association" title="Compact of Free Association">Compact of Free Association</a>, the U.S. is committed to provide US$57.7 million per year in assistance to the Marshall Islands (RMI) through 2013, and then US$62.7 million through 2023, at which time a trust fund, made up of U.S. and RMI contributions, will begin perpetual annual payouts.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-70"><a href="#cite_note-70">[68]</a></sup>\n</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Army" title="United States Army">United States Army</a> maintains the <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Reagan_Ballistic_Missile_Defense_Test_Site" title="Ronald Reagan Ballistic Missile Defense Test Site">Ronald Reagan Ballistic Missile Defense Test Site</a> on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kwajalein" title="Kwajalein">Kwajalein</a> Atoll. Marshallese land owners receive rent for the base.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Agriculture">Agriculture</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Agriculture">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Marshall_Islands_PICT0355_(4744730879).jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1920" data-file-width="2560" decoding="async" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Marshall_Islands_PICT0355_%284744730879%29.jpg/220px-Marshall_Islands_PICT0355_%284744730879%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Marshall_Islands_PICT0355_%284744730879%29.jpg/330px-Marshall_Islands_PICT0355_%284744730879%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Marshall_Islands_PICT0355_%284744730879%29.jpg/440px-Marshall_Islands_PICT0355_%284744730879%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Marshall_Islands_PICT0355_(4744730879).jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Coconut" title="Coconut">Coconut</a> palms in the Marshall Islands</div></div></div>\n<p>Agricultural production is concentrated on small farms.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-71"><a href="#cite_note-71">[69]</a></sup> The most important commercial crops is <a href="/wiki/Copra" title="Copra">Copra</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-72"><a href="#cite_note-72">[70]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-73"><a href="#cite_note-73">[71]</a></sup> followed by coconut, breadfruit, pandanus, banana, taro and arrowroot. The livestock consists primarily of pigs and chickens.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-74"><a href="#cite_note-74">[72]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imf.org_61-1"><a href="#cite_note-imf.org-61">[59]</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Industry">Industry</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Industry">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Small-scale industry is limited to handicrafts, fish processing, and <a href="/wiki/Copra" title="Copra">copra</a>.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Fishing">Fishing</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Fishing">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Majuro is the world\'s busiest <a href="/wiki/Tuna" title="Tuna">tuna</a> transshipment port in the world, with 704 transshipments totaling 444,393 tons in 2015.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-75"><a href="#cite_note-75">[73]</a></sup> Majuro is also a tuna processing center; the Pan Pacific Foods plant exports processed tuna to a number of countries, primarily the United States under the <a href="/wiki/Bumble_Bee_Foods" title="Bumble Bee Foods">Bumble Bee</a> brand.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-76"><a href="#cite_note-76">[74]</a></sup> Fishing license fees, primarily for tuna, provide noteworthy income for the government.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imf.org_61-2"><a href="#cite_note-imf.org-61">[59]</a></sup>\n</p><p>In 1999, a private company built a tuna loining plant with more than 400 employees, mostly women. But the plant closed in 2005 after a failed attempt to convert it to produce tuna steaks, a process that requires half as many employees. Operating costs exceeded revenue, and the plant\'s owners tried to partner with the government to prevent closure. But government officials personally interested in an economic stake in the plant refused to help. After the plant closed, it was taken over by the government, which had been the guarantor of a $2 million loan to the business.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (August 2015)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Energy">Energy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Energy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>On September 15, 2007, Witon Barry (of the Tobolar Copra processing plant in the Marshall Islands capital of <a href="/wiki/Majuro" title="Majuro">Majuro</a>) said power authorities, private companies, and entrepreneurs had been experimenting with <a href="/wiki/Coconut_oil" title="Coconut oil">coconut oil</a> as alternative to <a href="/wiki/Diesel_fuel" title="Diesel fuel">diesel fuel</a> for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vehicles" title="Vehicles">vehicles</a>, <a href="/wiki/Electricity_generation" title="Electricity generation">power generators</a>, and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ships" title="Ships">ships</a>. Coconut <a href="/wiki/Tree" title="Tree">trees</a> abound in the Pacific\'s <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tropical" title="Tropical">tropical</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Islands" title="Islands">islands</a>. <a href="/wiki/Copra" title="Copra">Copra</a>, the meat of the <a href="/wiki/Coconut" title="Coconut">coconut</a>, yields coconut oil (1 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Liter" title="Liter">liter</a> for every 6 to 10 coconuts).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-77"><a href="#cite_note-77">[75]</a></sup> In 2009, a 57&#160;kW <a href="/wiki/Solar_power" title="Solar power">solar power</a> plant was installed, the largest in the Pacific at the time, including New Zealand.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-78"><a href="#cite_note-78">[76]</a></sup> It is estimated that 330&#160;kW of solar and 450&#160;kW of wind power would be required to make the <a href="/wiki/College_of_the_Marshall_Islands" title="College of the Marshall Islands">College of the Marshall Islands</a> energy self-sufficient.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-79"><a href="#cite_note-79">[77]</a></sup> Marshalls Energy Company (MEC), a government entity, provides the islands with electricity. In 2008, 420 solar home systems of 200 Wp each were installed on Ailinglaplap Atoll, sufficient for limited electricity use.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-80"><a href="#cite_note-80">[78]</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Education">Education</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Education">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>The <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Education_(Marshall_Islands)" title="Ministry of Education (Marshall Islands)">Ministry of Education</a> is the education agency of the islands. <a href="/wiki/Marshall_Islands_Public_School_System" title="Marshall Islands Public School System">Marshall Islands Public School System</a> operates the state schools in the Marshall Islands.\n</p><p>In the 1994-1995 school year the country had 103 elementary schools and 13 secondary schools. There were 27 private elementary schools and 1 private high school. Christian groups operated most of the private schools.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-McMurrayetalp127_81-0"><a href="#cite_note-McMurrayetalp127-81">[79]</a></sup>\n</p><p>Historically the Marshallese population was taught in English first with Marshallese instruction coming later, but this was reversed in the 1990s to keep the islands\' cultural heritage and so children could write in Marshallese. Now English language instruction begins in grade 3. Christine McMurray and Roy Smith wrote in <i>Diseases of Globalization: Socioeconomic Transition and Health</i> that this could potentially weaken the children\'s English skills.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-McMurrayetalp127_81-1"><a href="#cite_note-McMurrayetalp127-81">[79]</a></sup>\n</p><p>There are two <a href="/wiki/Tertiary_education" title="Tertiary education">tertiary</a> institutions operating in the Marshall Islands, the <a href="/wiki/College_of_the_Marshall_Islands" title="College of the Marshall Islands">College of the Marshall Islands</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-82"><a href="#cite_note-82">[80]</a></sup> and the <a href="/wiki/University_of_the_South_Pacific" title="University of the South Pacific">University of the South Pacific</a>.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Transportation">Transportation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Transportation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Transportation_in_the_Marshall_Islands" title="Transportation in the Marshall Islands">Transportation in the Marshall Islands</a></div>\n<p>The Marshall Islands are served by the <a href="/wiki/Marshall_Islands_International_Airport" title="Marshall Islands International Airport">Marshall Islands International Airport</a> in Majuro, the <a href="/wiki/Bucholz_Army_Airfield" title="Bucholz Army Airfield">Bucholz Army Airfield</a> in Kwajalein, and <a href="/wiki/List_of_airports_in_the_Marshall_Islands" title="List of airports in the Marshall Islands">other small airports and airstrips</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-83"><a href="#cite_note-83">[81]</a></sup>\n</p><p>Airlines include <a href="/wiki/United_Airlines" title="United Airlines">United Airlines</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Our_Airline" title="Our Airline">Our Airline</a>, <a href="/wiki/Air_Marshall_Islands" title="Air Marshall Islands">Air Marshall Islands</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Asia_Pacific_Airlines_(United_States)" title="Asia Pacific Airlines (United States)">Asia Pacific Airlines</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-84"><a href="#cite_note-84">[82]</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Media_and_communications">Media and communications</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Media and communications">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>The Marshall Islands have several AM and FM radio stations. AM stations are 1098 5&#160;kW V7AB Majuro (Radio Marshalls, national coverage) and 1224 AFN Kwajalein (both public radio) as well as 1557 Micronesia Heatwave. The FM stations are 97.9 V7AD Majuro,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-85"><a href="#cite_note-85">[83]</a></sup> V7AA 96.3 FM Uliga<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-86"><a href="#cite_note-86">[84]</a></sup> and 104.1 V7AA Majuro (Baptist religious). BBC World is broadcast on 98.5 FM Majuro.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ReferenceA_87-0"><a href="#cite_note-ReferenceA-87">[85]</a></sup> The most recent station is Power 103.5 which started broadcasting in 2016.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-88"><a href="#cite_note-88">[86]</a></sup>\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/American_Forces_Network" title="American Forces Network">AFRTS</a> stations include 99.9 AFN Kwajalein (country), 101.1 AFN (adult rock) and 102.1 AFN (hot AC).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-89"><a href="#cite_note-89">[87]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-90"><a href="#cite_note-90">[88]</a></sup>\n</p><p>There is one broadcast television station, MBC-TV operated by the state.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-91"><a href="#cite_note-91">[89]</a></sup> Cable TV is available. On cable TV, most programs are shown two weeks later than in North America but news in real time can be viewed on CNN, CNBC and BBC.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-92"><a href="#cite_note-92">[90]</a></sup> American Forces Radio and Television also provides TV service to Kwajalein Atoll.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-93"><a href="#cite_note-93">[91]</a></sup>\n</p><p>The Marshall Islands National Telecommunications Authority (NTA) provides telephone, cable TV (MHTV), FAX, cellular and Internet services.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-94"><a href="#cite_note-94">[92]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-95"><a href="#cite_note-95">[93]</a></sup> The Authority is a private corporation with significant ownership by the national government.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-96"><a href="#cite_note-96">[94]</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">See also</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marshall_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: See also">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div aria-label="Portals" class="noprint portal plainlist tright" role="navigation" style="margin:0.5em 0 0.5em 1em;border:solid #aaa 1px">\n<ul Files</a></i></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Visa_policy_of_the_Marshall_Islands" title="Visa policy of the Marshall Islands">Visa policy of the Marshall Islands</a></li></ul>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="cite_note-6"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-6">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Pronunciations:<br/>* <a href="/wiki/English_language" title="English Islands.ogg">listen</a></span></span>)</span></span><br/>* <a href="/wiki/Marshallese_language" title="Marshallese language">Marshallese</a>: <i><i lang="mh" title="Marshallese language title="Help:IPA/Marshallese">[&#593;&#815;&#593;&#865;&#594;&#596;&#815;&#596;&#865;&#603;l&#690;&#603;b&#690;&#230;n&#690;&#160;&#593;&#815;&#593;&#865;&#594;o&#815;o&#865;&#612;r&#736;&#612;&#609;&#623;&#865;in&#690;&#160;m&#736;&#593;&#593;&#815;z&#690;&#603;&#865;&#652;&#619;]</a></span>)</span>\n</li>\n<li id="cite_note-7"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-7">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="/wiki/Wake_Island" title="Wake Island">Wake Island</a> is claimed as a territory of the Marshall Islands, but is also claimed as an <a href="/wiki/Unorganized_territory" title="Unorganized territory">unorganized</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Unincorporated_territory" title="Unincorporated territory">unincorporated territory</a> of the United States, with <i>de facto</i> control vested in the <a href="/wiki/Office_of_Insular_Affairs" title="Office of Insular Affairs">Office of Insular Affairs</a> (and all military defenses managed by the United States
